# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     7→	"bytes"

     9→	"sort"
    10→
    11→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    13→)
    14→
    15→// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
    16→// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level
    17→// detail.
    18→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    19→
    20→// Format returns a compact diff summary of the given plan. It outputs one line
    21→// per resource change in the format "[action] resource_type.name", groups
    22→// changes by action type, and shows summary counts at the end.
    23→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    24→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    25→		return ""
    26→	}
    27→
    28→	var buf bytes.Buffer
    29→
    30→	// Group resources by action
    31→	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
    32→	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
    33→		changesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)
    34→	}
    35→
    36→	// Define the order of actions for output
    37→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    38→		plans.Create,
    39→		plans.Update,
    40→		plans.Delete,
    41→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    42→		plans.CreateThenDelete,
    43→		plans.Read,
    44→		plans.Forget,
    45→		plans.CreateThenForget,
    46→		plans.NoOp,
    47→	}
    48→
    49→	// Track counts
    50→	counts := make(map[plans.Action]int)
    51→
    52→	// Output changes grouped by action
    53→	for _, action := range actionOrder {

... (truncated)

// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level
// detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact diff summary of the given plan. It outputs one line
// per resource change in the format "[action] resource_type.name", groups
// changes by action type, and shows summary counts at the end.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	var buf bytes.Buffer

	// Group resources by action
	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		changesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)
	}

	// Define the order of actions for output
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.NoOp,
	}

	// Track counts
	counts := make(map[plans.Action]int)
95-assistanttool_useBash
96-usertool_resultBash
			resourceName := addr.Resource.Resource.Name

			// Format the output line
			symbol := DiffActionSymbol(change.Action)
			buf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s.%s\n", symbol, resourceType, resourceName))
			counts[action]++
		}
	}

	// Add summary counts
	if len(counts) > 0 {
		buf.WriteString("\nSummary:\n")

		totalAdded := counts[plans.Create] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]
		totalChanged := counts[plans.Update] + counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]
		totalDestroyed := counts[plans.Delete] + counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]

		if totalAdded > 0 {
			buf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("  + %d resource(s) added\n", totalAdded))
		}
		if totalChanged > 0 {
			buf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("  ~ %d resource(s) changed\n", totalChanged))
		}
		if totalDestroyed > 0 {
			buf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("  - %d resource(s) destroyed\n", totalDestroyed))
		}
	}

	return buf.String()
}

It outputs one line\n// per resource change in the format \"[action] resource_type.name\", groups\n// changes by action type, and shows summary counts at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tchangesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for output\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\t// changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Output each change\n\t\tfor _, change := range changes {\n\t\t\taddr := change.Addr\n\t\t\tresourceType := addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := addr.Resource.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Format the output line\n\t\t\tsymbol := DiffActionSymbol(change.Action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s.%s\\n\", symbol, resourceType, resourceName))\n\t\t\tcounts[action]++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add summary counts\n\tif len(counts) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\nSummary:\\n\")\n\n\t\ttotalAdded := counts[plans.Create] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]\n\t\ttotalChanged := counts[plans.Update] + counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]\n\t\ttotalDestroyed := counts[plans.Delete] + counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]\n\n\t\tif totalAdded > 0 {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  + %d resource(s) added\\n\", totalAdded))\n\t\t}\n\t\tif totalChanged > 0 {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  ~ %d resource(s) changed\\n\", totalChanged))\n\t\t}\n\t\tif totalDestroyed > 0 {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  - %d resource(s) destroyed\\n\", totalDestroyed))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n",

It outputs one line\n// per resource change in the format \"[action] resource_type.name\", groups\n// changes by action type, and shows summary counts at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter)         Code Changes (2)
        
1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level
// detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact diff summary of the given plan. It outputs one line
// per resource change in the format "[action] resource_type.name", groups
// changes by action type, and shows summary counts at the end.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	var buf bytes.Buffer

	// Group resources by action
	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		changesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)
	}

	// Define the order of actions for output
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.NoOp,
	}

	// Track counts
	counts := make(map[plans.Action]int)

	// Output changes grouped by action
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		changes, ok := changesByAction[action]
		if !ok || len(changes) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Sort changes by address for consistent output
		sort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {
			return changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()
		})

		// Output each change
		for _, change := range changes {
			addr := change.Addr
			resourceType := addr.Resource.Res
